must this word means that the statement is an absolute mandate 400 u must not this phrase means that the statement is an absolut prohibition 401 u should this word means that there may exist valid reasons in particular circumstances 402 to ignore the statement but the full implications must be understood and carefully weighed 403 before choosing different course 404 u should not this phrase means that there may exist valid reaso ns in particular 405 circumstances to implement or accept the behavior d escribed in the statement but the full 406 implications must first be understood and carefully weighed 407 u may or optional these words means that compliance with the stateme nt is optional 408 kmi 2200 vol 2 unclassifiedfor official use only 30 sept 2005 security policy and related
